msg:Poor hygiene, poor service, but the worst attitude towards solving problems!
To be honest, this is not my first time staying at Zhanyun Hotel. I have stayed there before and it was pretty good, but this time it made me feel sick.
1. When I first checked in, I asked for a drink of water. I found that the cupboard where there should be cups was empty. Did you clear the room before? I thought I'd make do with it. I'd use a toothbrush cup to wash my teeth and drink water first. Then the cleaning staff would wash the cup the next day. Will they refill it for me then? Unfortunately, I overthought it and came back the next day still empty. This shows two problems with this hotel. First, after cleaning up the room for the previous guest, there was no minimum reset and inspection of items, so it was passed by in a fool's errand. Second, I didn‚Äôt clean the room seriously and didn‚Äôt follow the basic procedures. Otherwise, if this situation didn‚Äôt happen, how would you say the cleaning was just passable? Can you rest assured?
2. I went to bed very tired when I arrived that day, but the next day I found a yellow travel shoe sole mark on the sheets under the pillow! Isn't this too exaggerated? I slept on it all night! This is too disgusting! Thinking about it carefully, I couldn't see it because the pillow was covering it. So couldn't the staff see it? There's no way they couldn't have seen it when they tidied up the last room, right? If you don't see it, you haven't changed the bed sheets and pillowcases. If you don't change it if you see it...is it intentional? Also, if you look closely, there are yellow marks on the sheets. What are they? Did you feel disgusted after watching it? Do you dare to sleep in a hotel like this?
3. The wash basin. After these two things, I suddenly became very worried about the hygiene of the hotel. Look carefully, there are many yellow dots on the top of the wash basin. This is a cleaned wash basin. What are these yellow marks? I can‚Äôt even think about it, it makes me sick!
4. The above problems are about hygiene, inadequate cleaning and lax management, but the subsequent problem is about attitude and how a hotel faces its customers. I slept all night on sheets with footprints and yellow spots, drank water without a cup, and used a sink with yellow marks. I was in a very bad mood. I went to the front desk to communicate with them. Such poor hygiene and such a terrible stay experience, I asked for a one-night discount. The room charge is not exorbitant, right? It's not impossible for me to go to the health depar**ent and report it with the photos and ask for compensation. But what about their answer: Can I give you a fruit plate? No, can I give you breakfast? Or upgrade a room? Do you want more? Then you are making unreasonable demands!
For the deputy front office manager who solves the problem, it is reasonable if he can get through it with a little effort, and it is unreasonable if he has to go through a lot of effort to reduce or reduce some money. How fair.
Whether a hotel is good or bad, facilities are only secondary, health and service are fundamental. This hotel has bedsheets with shoe prints and yellow spots, a sink with yellow prints, and a front office manager with a tough attitude, but there is no drinking glass.
Don't come, you will suffer.
